NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
We hereby state that the male child Mani, born on 20-10-2013 is an inmate of Christ Faith Home For Children
3/91, Mettu Colony, Manapakkam, Chennai-600 125. Child Mani has been adopted by Mr. Ralph John Sequeira and
Mrs. Melrine Babita Sequeira. Resident of 11, Millcar Drive, Toronto, Ontario, MIB 6J6, Represented by Power of Attorney
Agent, Mrs. Sunitha Joe, No. 3/91, Mettu Colony, Manapakkam, Chennai-600 125. That the Adoption order was granted
by the Hon’ble Judge Mr. Justice R. Subbiah, High Court of Judicature at Madras on 23-12-2014 in O.P. No. 784/2014.
Now adopted parents wanted to change the name of the child from MANI to NATHAN JOHN SEQUEIRA. Henceforth the
child name may be called as NATHAN JOHN SEQUEIRA.

MRS. SUNITHA JOE,
Power of Attorney Agent.
For Adoptive Parents,
Mr. Ralph John Sequeira,
Mrs. Melrine Babita Sequeira.

Chennai,
2nd March 2015.

PACIFIC AUTOMOTIVE INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
Registered Office: New No. 39, First Main Road, R.A. Puram, Chennai, Tamil Nadu-600 028.
(Publication in pursuance of Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956)
Notice is hereby given in general information that the members of M/S PACIFIC AUTOMOTIVE INDIA PRIVATE
LIMITED at its Extra-Ordinary General Meeting of the Company held on Saturday, the 28th day of February, 2015 at its
Registered Office No. 39, First Main Road, R.A. Puram, Chennai, Tamil Nadu-600 028, India have passed the following
special resolution to wind up the above Company voluntarily:
“RESOLVED THAT in terms of the provisions of Section 484 (1)(b) and other applicable provisions, if any, of the
Companies Act, 1956, the consent of shareholders of the company be and is hereby accorded for voluntary winding up of
the Company as Member’s Voluntary Winding up.”

By Order of the Board

DIN: 02174600
Chennai,
6th March 2015.

HIMANSHU SRIVASTAVA,
